 ------------

 Jello shots
 
 Ingredients:
 2 cups Everclear , 190 proof
 3 packages Jello with sugar
 3 cups Water
 Mixing instructions:
 Boil 3 cups of water then add jello. Mix jello and water until jello is
  completely disolved. Add the two cups of everclear and mix together.
  Pour mixture into plastic shot glasses and chill until firm. Then, eat
  away...
 Serve in: Shot glass.
 
 ------------

 Jose Cuervo Gold Shooter
  Materials Needed:
   Shaker or Packet of Salt
   Wedge of Lime
   30 ml. measure of José Cuervo Gold in a shotglass
  Method:
   Lick the back of the hollow of the hand (between the thumb and
   forefinger) and sprinkle salt on the area. Then lick the salt from
   the hand and drink the shot of José Cuervo tequila all in one swallow.
   Immediately bite the wedge of lime to complete the taste and ritual

 Jose Cuervo Gold Slammer
  Materials Needed:
   Measure of José Cuervo Gold in a shotglass
   7-Up, Sprite, Fizzy lemonade or carbonated sweet beverage
  Method:
   Pour a measure of Jose Curevo Gold into a shotglass leaving enough
   room to top it off with the sweet, carbonated beverage. Once two are
   poured, place a napkin or your hand over the top of the shot glass as
   not to spill the contents. Slam down the glass, mixing and fizzing the
   contents. Drink quickly before contents bubble over or returns to
   normal state. 

 The Jose Cuervo Frog
  Materials Needed:
   Bottle of Corona
   Wedge of fresh, juicy lime
   30 ml. measure of José Cuervo
  Method:
   Drink just enough beer to make room for the 30 ml. measure of Jose
   Cuervo Gold. Pour the shot of José Cuervo Gold into the neck of the
   Corona beer. Take the wedge of lime and squeeze the juice into the neck
   until the liquid in the neck appears foggy. The objective is to drink
   the Corona down to the Corona name on the bottle. Once the first shot
   is consumed, the end result is a pleasant taste of José Cuervo Gold
   lingering in the rest of the Corona beer. 
 
 Jose Cuervo Montana Shooter
  Materials Needed:
   Shaker or packet of salt
   Wedge of fresh, juicy lime
   30 ml. measure of José Cuervo Gold in a shotglass
  Method:
   Place the wedge of lime on the table. Pick up the salt shaker, sprinkle
   it over your shoulder, shoot the José Cuervo Gold, then slam your fist
   on the wedge of lime. 

 Jose Cuervo Gold Margarita
  45 ml. José Cuervo Especial
  30 ml. Cointreau
  90-120 ml. Sweet & Sour
   Squeeze 1/2 fresh lime into the drink. Garnish with a fresh lime wedge. 

 Jose Cuervo Gold Margarita
  45 ml. José Cuervo Especial
  30 ml. Triple Sec
  30 ml. Lime Juice
  1/2 cup Frozen Strawberries
   In blender, combine all ingredients with ice. Pour into glass. Garnish
   with fresh strawberry. 

 Jose Cuervo Spike
  45 ml. José Cuervo Especial
  Grapefruit juice to fill
   Pour José Cuervo Especial over ice in a tall glass, add grapefruit
   juice, stir and server. Garnish with a fresh orange wedge. 


 Jose Cuervo Sunrise 
  45 ml. José Cuervo Especial
  15 ml. Lime Juice
  90 ml. Orange Juice
  15 ml. Genadine
   Mix ingredients then pour Grenadine to create sunrise.

 Jack Daniel's Country Cocktails recipes:

 Lynchburg Lemonade
 1 part Jack Daniel's Tennessee Whiskey
 1 part triple sec
 1 part sweet and sour mix
 2 parts lemon-lime soda
 
 Hurricane Punch
 1 part Jack Daniel's Tennessee Whiskey
 1 part dark rum
 2 parts orange juice
 1 part grenadine
 1 part lemon-lime soda
 
 Wildberry Jack
 1 part Jack Daniel's Tennessee Whiskey
 1 part berry flavored schnapps
 2 parts cranberry juice
 2 parts lemon-lime soda
 1/4 part simple syrup (2 teaspoons sugar)
 
 Downhome Punch
 1 part Jack Daniel's Tennessee Whiskey
 1 part peach schnapps
 2 parts sweet and sour mix
 2 parts orange juice
 top with Sloe Gin
 
 AppleJack
 1 part Jack Daniel's Tennessee Whiskey
 2 parts sour apple schnapps
 1 part sweet and sour mix
 1 part club soda
 Bitters to taste
 
 Watermelon Spike
 1 part Jack Daniel's Tennessee Whiskey
 1 1/2 parts watermelon liqueur
 1/2 part melon liqueur
 2 parts lemon-lime soda
 1/4 part grenadine
 
 Red-Eyed Jack
 1 part Jack Daniel's Tennessee Whiskey
 1/2 part amaretto
 4 parts cranberry juice
 
 Tennessee Tea
 1 part Jack Daniel's Tennessee Whiskey
 1 part whiskey sour mix
 1 part triple sec
 2 parts cola
 
 Blackberry Jack
 1 part Jack Daniel's Tennessee Whiskey
 1 part blackberry brandy
 2 parts lemon-lime soda
 1/4 part grenadine
 
 Cactus Kicker
 1 part Jack Daniel's Tennessee Whiskey
 1/2 part Pepe Lopez Tequila
 1/2 part sweet and sour mix
 1/4 part sweetened lime juice
 1 part lemon-lime soda
 Rim glass with salt and garnish with lime.

 FLAMEING DR. PEPPER

 151 Rum (float small amount on top)

 Flaming Mike's 
 3/4 shot Peach Schnapps
 1/4 shot Absolute Citron
 dash 151 rum
 drop of cherry cough syrup
 *******Pour the peach schnapps into a shot glass, folowed by the Citron.
 Top with a small amount of 151 rum. Then put in one drop of cherry
 cough syrup. Light the shot and let it warm up for 20-30 seconds.
 Blow out the flame and drink.  * Sounds kind of funny, but this is
 a drink you should try. * Be careful that the shot glass does not
 touch your lips.*******

 1 oz cherry mix \ 1/3 sweet sour mix \\ 2/3 orange juice 
 ice (shake) \ rocks \ (for flavors leave out cherry mix)
 Add 2 oz flavor mix or Schnapps for a Cherry, 
 Peach, Blackberry, Raspberry, Strawberry, or 
 Wildberry Grape Fifty Seven Chevy

 2 oz Coconut Rum 
 fill orange juice \ 1 oz cream 
 ice \ rocks 
 or frozen (add 2 scoops ice cream or mix) 
 Add 2 oz flavor mix or Schnapps for a Cherry, 
 Peach, Blackberry, Raspberry, Strawberry, or 
 Wildberry Malibu Sherbert

 Ride The Wave
 (Shot)
 1 part ABSOLUT
 1 part Malibu Rum
 1 Part Amaretto 

 Romulan Ale 
 150 ml Everclear
 150 ml Blue Curacao
 150 ml Bacardi 151 Rum
 12 ounces Sprite
 1) Grab a cool, old, glass bottle (something that you can throw
  in the freezer).
 2) Pour all the Everclear, Blue Curacao, and Bacardi into the
  bottle.
 3) Throw the bottle in the freezer until you just can't take it
  anymore.
 4) Pour one ounce of the pretty, blue concoction into a tall
  glass.
 5) Fill with Sprite and ice and you're in for one hell of an
  evening!
